Short 2-write binary WOM code list

On this page, a list of known 2-write binary WOM codes is composed, in most cases together with their definition. Only individual code instances are included, no constructions containing free parameters. Main reason for creation was to have some way to get an overview which codes have been found, how they are defined and how they compare to other codes. In order to determine lower bounds to OEIS terms, the individually found known and unknown write number codes are combined to new codes in a trivial way. These are called 'derived' codes. The adjective 'short' is of course quite imprecise. The codes based on an arbitrary decoding map need to be stored in a practical table, and the 1st write vectors of codes based on coset coding need to be enumerated in a reasonable time.

The page is organised in three tables:

  • List of WOM codes with unknown write number
  • List of WOM codes with known write number
  • List of derived WOM codes

List of 2-write WOM codes (known write number), including derived:

In the table below, the following observation is exploited:

If we have two unrestricted rate 2-write WOM codes of dimensions <a1,a2>/n and <b1,b2>/m , and the write number is known,
we can write the codes next to eachother and use this as a code of size < (a1·b1) , (a2·b2) > / (n+m)

The table shows per code length the codes that are not outperformed by others in terms of 1st and 2nd write symbol count.

The cells in green show the maximum fixed and unrestricted coding rate obtained per code length.
